CalWatch crashed around 9pm (21:08:11) tonight but came back again working just fine. The actual
failure appeared to happen at 20:52:45, where we tripped the whole redraw-loop-while-drawthread-is-null
Heisenbug, threw an uncaught exception, and blew up.

For now:
- enhanced the Zombie cleanup mechanism in MyTimeListener
- we need to find out why drawThread is being set to null without the drawThread itself dying
  - best current theory: killDrawThread() isn't actually working
  - kludgy workaround: all the zombie code is now super enhanced

- However, it seems that this particular crash was just that the logic in redrawClock(String) was
  buggy. The case for calling redrawInternal didn't allow for cases when we're not drawingMaxHertz
  yet nor are we drawingAmbientMode. Which is to say, all of the "slow" redraw cases. The fix
  there is to add source != null. Now, the only time we'll hopefully ever trigger all the zombie logic
  is when we're on a "fast" redraw.
